{"type":"assistant","message":{"model":"claude-haiku-4-5-20251001","id":"msg_011syTVHhTVnYidZcCLgmms9","type":"message","role":"assistant","content":[{"type":"tool_use","id":"toolu_019181EsKcU827XY5fY9dEZo","name":"Write","input":{"file_path":"/workspace/documentation.md","content":"# Envoy HTTP Connection Manager Architecture\n\n## Overview\n\nThe HTTP Connection Manager (HCM) is Envoy's core subsystem for processing HTTP requests from downstream clients through to upstream services. This document explains how the major components interact to handle HTTP request/response lifecycle: from receiving raw bytes on a downstream connection, through per-stream filtering and routing, to dispatching upstream requests and returning responses downstream.\n\nThe architecture consists of four tightly-integrated layers:\n\n1. **ConnectionManagerImpl** — Network I/O and connection lifecycle management\n2. **FilterManager** — Per-stream filter chain execution engine\n3. **Router Filter** — Terminal filter that performs route selection and upstream dispatch\n4. **Cluster Manager** — Upstream connection pool allocation and host selection\n\n---\n\n## 1. ConnectionManagerImpl: Network Read Filter and Connection Lifecycle\n\n**Source files:**\n- `source/common/http/conn_manager_impl.h` (lines 60-220)\n- `source/common/http/conn_manager_impl.cc` (lines 118-300)\n\n### Responsibilities\n\nConnectionManagerImpl is a `Network::ReadFilter` that owns the HTTP connection lifecycle. It:\n\n- **Receives raw downstream bytes** via the `Network::ReadFilter` interface's `onData()` method\n- **Instantiates and manages the HTTP codec** (H1/H2/H3) lazily based on the first bytes received\n- **Creates and tracks `ActiveStream` objects** — one per HTTP request/response pair\n- **Manages connection-level concerns**:\n  - Drain decisions (graceful shutdown)\n  - Overload management (rejecting new streams under load)\n  - Write buffer watermarks (pausing/resuming downstream read when buffers exceed limits)\n  - Connection lifetime limits (max requests, timeouts)\n  - Tracing and access logging coordination\n\n### Key Data Structures\n\n```cpp\nclass ConnectionManagerImpl :\n    public Network::ReadFilter,           // Implements onData()\n    public ServerConnectionCallbacks,     // Codec callbacks\n    public Network::ConnectionCallbacks   // Connection events\n{\nprivate:\n    struct ActiveStream : LinkedObject<ActiveStream>,     // Linked list node\n                         public FilterManagerCallbacks,   // Filter manager interface\n                         public StreamCallbacks          // Stream callbacks\n    {\n        // Per-stream state:\n        RequestHeaderMapSharedPtr request_headers_;\n        ResponseHeaderMapPtr response_headers_;\n        uint32_t stream_id_;\n        FilterManager filter_manager_;                    // Stream's filter chain\n        // ... additional stream state\n    };\n\n    ServerConnectionPtr codec_;           // HTTP codec (created lazily)\n    std::list<ActiveStream> active_streams_;  // Linked list of streams\n    Network::ReadFilterCallbacks* read_callbacks_;\n};\n```\n\n### Connection Lifecycle: From Bytes to Streams\n\n#### 1. Connection Established\n```\nNetwork → onNewConnection()\n  ├─ Register connection callbacks with Network::Connection\n  └─ Defer codec creation (H1/H2 wait for first bytes, H3 creates immediately)\n```\n\n#### 2. Downstream Bytes Arrive\n```\nNetwork → onData(Buffer::Instance& data)\n  ├─ Check if codec exists; if not, createCodec(data)\n  │   └─ Codec creation:\n  │       ├─ Inspect first bytes to determine protocol\n  │       ├─ Instantiate Http1CodecImpl, Http2CodecImpl, or Http3CodecImpl\n  │       └─ Register this as ServerConnectionCallbacks\n  │\n  └─ Dispatch data to codec:\n      codec_->dispatch(data)\n          └─ Codec parses frames and calls newStream() for each request\n```\n\n#### 3. Codec Signals New Request\n```\nCodec → newStream(ResponseEncoder& response_encoder)\n  ├─ Create ActiveStream in active_streams_ list\n  ├─ Allocate RequestDecoder interface from ActiveStream\n  └─ Return RequestDecoder to codec\n      └─ Codec calls decoder→decodeHeaders(), decodeData(), decodeTrailers()\n```\n\n### ActiveStream: Per-Stream Filtering and Response\n\nEach `ActiveStream`:\n\n- **Acts as RequestDecoder**: Receives decoded headers/data/trailers from the codec\n- **Owns a FilterManager**: Manages the per-stream filter chain\n- **Implements FilterManagerCallbacks**: Callbacks from FilterManager to coordinate response sending\n- **Implements StreamCallbacks**: Receives codec-level events (reset, watermarks)\n\n```cpp\nstruct ActiveStream : RequestDecoder, FilterManagerCallbacks {\n\n    // From codec: decoded request data\n    void decodeHeaders(RequestHeaderMapSharedPtr&& headers, bool end_stream) {\n        filter_manager_.decodeHeaders(*headers, end_stream);  // Send through filter chain\n    }\n\n    void decodeData(Buffer::Instance& data, bool end_stream) {\n        filter_manager_.decodeData(data, end_stream);         // Send through filter chain\n    }\n\n    void decodeTrailers(RequestTrailerMapPtr&& trailers) {\n        filter_manager_.decodeTrailers(*trailers);           // Send through filter chain\n    }\n\n    // From filter chain: response to send\n    void encodeHeaders(ResponseHeaderMapPtr&& headers, bool end_stream) override {\n        response_encoder_->encodeHeaders(*headers, end_stream);  // Codec encodes to wire\n    }\n};\n```\n\n### Connection-Level Concerns\n\n#### Overload Management\n- Before accepting a new stream, check `OverloadManager::isOverloaded()`\n- If overloaded, send local reply with 503 Service Unavailable\n- Prevents unbounded stream accumulation under load\n\n#### Drain Decision\n- Checks `Network::DrainDecision` at connection level\n- When draining, sends GOAWAY (HTTP/2) or closes after final response\n- Allows graceful load balancer-initiated shutdown\n\n#### Write Buffer Watermarking\n```\nFilter chain buffers response → watermark high\n  └─ Codec's write buffer exceeds limit\n      └─ ConnectionManagerImpl→onAboveWriteBufferHighWatermark()\n          └─ codec_→onUnderlyingConnectionAboveWriteBufferHighWatermark()\n              └─ Pauses new stream reads\n\nCodec flushes buffer → watermark low\n  └─ ConnectionManagerImpl→onBelowWriteBufferLowWatermark()\n      └─ codec_→onUnderlyingConnectionBelowWriteBufferLowWatermark()\n          └─ Resumes new stream reads\n```\n\n---\n\n## 2. FilterManager and HTTP Filter Chain\n\n**Source files:**\n- `source/common/http/filter_manager.h` (lines 679-850)\n- `source/common/http/filter_manager.cc`\n\n### Responsibilities\n\nFilterManager is the per-stream **filter chain execution engine**. It:\n\n- **Creates the filter chain** via `FilterChainFactory::createFilterChain()` for each new stream\n- **Routes data through decoder filters** (request path: headers → data → trailers)\n- **Routes data through encoder filters** (response path: same, in reverse order)\n- **Manages filter state transitions**: continuing, stopping, buffering, resuming\n- **Handles local replies**: sending error responses without involving upstream\n- **Coordinates watermarks**: pausing iteration when filters buffer data\n\n### Filter Chain Structure\n\n```cpp\n// Decoder filter chain: A → B → C (in configured order)\nstruct StreamDecoderFilters {\n    std::vector<ActiveStreamDecoderFilterPtr> entries_;  // A, B, C\n    Iterator begin() { return entries_.begin(); }       // Iterates A→B→C\n};\n\n// Encoder filter chain: A → B → C (in reverse order)\nstruct StreamEncoderFilters {\n    std::vector<ActiveStreamEncoderFilterPtr> entries_;  // A, B, C\n    using Iterator = reverse_iterator;\n    Iterator begin() { return entries_.rbegin(); }      // Iterates C→B→A\n};\n```\n\n**Why reverse iteration for encoder?**\nData flows: `Router → FilterN → … → Filter1 → Codec`\nEach layer can modify/observe response before it reaches prior layers.\nTerminal filter (Router) is executed last on the way out, giving it last chance to modify response.\n\n### Request Path: decodeHeaders → decodeData → decodeTrailers\n\n```\ndecodeHeaders(headers, end_stream=false)\n  └─ FilterManager::decodeHeaders()\n      ├─ Iterate decoder_filters: [A, B, C, Router]\n      │   ├─ A.decodeHeaders(headers) → Continue\n      │   ├─ B.decodeHeaders(headers) → Continue\n      │   ├─ C.decodeHeaders(headers) → Continue\n      │   └─ Router.decodeHeaders(headers) → [router selects upstream]\n      │\n      └─ If headers indicate end_stream=true, send to downstream now\n\ndecodeData(data, end_stream=false)\n  └─ FilterManager::decodeData()\n      ├─ Iterate decoder_filters: [A, B, C, Router]\n      │   ├─ A.decodeData(data) → Continue (or buffer)\n      │   ├─ B.decodeData(data) → Continue\n      │   ├─ C.decodeData(data) → Continue\n      │   └─ Router.decodeData(data) → [forward to upstream]\n      │\n      └─ If end_stream=true, downstream request complete\n\ndecodeTrailers(trailers)\n  └─ Similar to decodeData, Router.decodeTrailers() signals upstream completion\n```\n\n### Response Path: encodeHeaders → encodeData → encodeTrailers\n\n```\n[Upstream sends response]\n  └─ UpstreamRequest.decodeHeaders(response_headers, end_stream=false)\n      └─ FilterManager (upstream direction).encodeHeaders()\n          ├─ Iterate encoder_filters in reverse: [Router, C, B, A]\n          │   ├─ Router.encodeHeaders(response_headers) → Continue\n          │   ├─ C.encodeHeaders(response_headers) → Continue\n          │   ├─ B.encodeHeaders(response_headers) → Continue\n          │   └─ A.encodeHeaders(response_headers) → Continue\n          │\n          └─ Call response_encoder_→encodeHeaders() [Codec encodes to wire]\n\n[Similarly for encodeData, encodeTrailers]\n```\n\n### Filter Return Values and Control Flow\n\nEach filter's callback returns a status that controls iteration:\n\n```cpp\nenum class FilterHeadersStatus {\n    Continue,              // Call next filter immediately\n    StopIteration,         // Stop, wait for resumption\n    StopIterationAndWatermark,  // Stop + inform FilterManager to apply watermarks\n    ContinueAndEndStream,  // Final headers already sent downstream\n};\n\nenum class FilterDataStatus {\n    Continue,              // Call next filter immediately\n    StopIteration,         // Buffer data, wait for resumption\n    StopIterationAndWatermark,  // Stop + apply backpressure\n    Continue,              // (no change)\n};\n```\n\n### Example: Router Filter Handling\n\nWhen Router filter's `decodeHeaders()` is called:\n1. Selects route based on request headers (domain, path, etc.)\n2. Looks up cluster from route\n3. Initiates upstream request creation asynchronously\n4. Returns `StopIteration` — waits for upstream to provide response encoder\n5. Once upstream pool provides encoder:\n   - Resumes remaining filters if any were stopped\n   - Continues with `decodeData` and `decodeTrailers` from downstream\n\nIf Router encounters an error (no cluster found, cluster unhealthy):\n- Calls `sendLocalReply(503, \"Cluster not found\")`\n- This **short-circuits the filter chain** — no upstream request is made\n- Response is encoded directly via downstream codec\n\n### Buffering and Watermarks\n\nWhen a filter returns `StopIterationAndWatermark`:\n\n```cpp\n// Filter busy, can't process more data\nreturn FilterDataStatus::StopIterationAndWatermark;\n\n// FilterManager:\n// 1. Buffers the provided_data in filter's internal buffer\n// 2. Calls FilterManager callbacks to signal high watermark upstream\n// 3. Downstream codec pauses reads\n// 4. When filter is ready: resumeIteration() → re-inject buffered data\n\n// Filter later calls: resumeIteration()\n// → FilterManager re-injects buffered data to next filter\n// → If all filters pass, eventually reaches codec or upstream\n```\n\n### Extension Points\n\nUsers extend HTTP handling via:\n\n1. **StreamDecoderFilter**: Sees request, can modify headers/body, optionally stop iteration\n   - Example: rate limiting filter, header manipulation\n2. **StreamEncoderFilter**: Sees response, can modify status/headers/body\n   - Example: response header addition, body compression\n3. **StreamFilter**: Both decoder and encoder (single object for bidirectional processing)\n   - Example: tracing filter, logging filter\n\n```cpp\n// Custom filter registration in HCM config:\nhttp_filters:\n  - name: envoy.filters.http.router\n    typed_config:\n      \"@type\": type.googleapis.com/envoy.extensions.filters.http.router.v3.Router\n      upstream_http_filters:\n        - name: my-custom-filter\n```\n\n---\n\n## 3. Router Filter: Route Selection and Upstream Dispatch\n\n**Source files:**\n- `source/common/router/router.h` (lines 1-300)\n- `source/common/router/router.cc` (lines 1-400)\n- `source/common/router/upstream_request.h` (lines 67-200)\n\n### Responsibilities\n\nThe Router filter is the **terminal decoder filter** that:\n\n- **Selects a route** from `RouteConfiguration` based on request headers\n- **Picks a cluster** from the matched route\n- **Initiates upstream request creation** via ClusterManager\n- **Manages request lifecycle**: retry logic, timeouts, shadowing\n- **Handles upstream response**: passes response back through filter chain (encoder direction)\n\n### Request Processing: decodeHeaders\n\n```cpp\nclass Filter : public StreamDecoderFilter {\n    FilterHeadersStatus decodeHeaders(RequestHeaderMap& headers, bool end_stream) {\n        // 1. Route selection\n        route_entry_ = config_->routeConfig().route(headers, ...);\n        if (!route_entry_) {\n            sendLocalReply(Http::Code::NotFound, \"no matching route\");\n            return FilterHeadersStatus::StopIteration;\n        }\n\n        // 2. Cluster selection\n        cluster_ = route_entry_->clusterName();\n\n        // 3. Load balancer context setup\n        // (provides metadata match criteria, etc.)\n\n        // 4. Initiate upstream request\n        upstream_request_ = std::make_unique<UpstreamRequest>(\n            *this,\n            cluster_manager_.getThreadLocalCluster(cluster_)->connPool(...),\n            can_send_early_data_, can_use_http3_, enable_half_close\n        );\n\n        // 5. Pass headers to upstream pool\n        upstream_request_->acceptHeadersFromRouter(end_stream);\n\n        return FilterHeadersStatus::StopIteration;  // Wait for upstream pool\n    }\n};\n```\n\n### UpstreamRequest: Upstream Lifecycle\n\nUpstreamRequest (in `source/common/router/upstream_request.h`) manages the upstream side:\n\n```cpp\nclass UpstreamRequest {\n    // Connection pool obtained from cluster\n    std::unique_ptr<GenericConnPool> conn_pool_;\n\n    // Upstream encoder (once connection is ready)\n    Http::RequestEncoder* upstream_encoder_{nullptr};\n\n    // Filter manager for upstream-side filters\n    std::unique_ptr<Http::FilterManager> upstream_filter_manager_;\n\npublic:\n    // Called by router with downstream request data\n    void acceptHeadersFromRouter(bool end_stream) {\n        conn_pool_->newStream(*this);  // Async: calls onPoolReady() or onPoolFailure()\n    }\n\n    void acceptDataFromRouter(Buffer::Instance& data, bool end_stream) {\n        if (upstream_encoder_) {\n            upstream_encoder_->encodeData(data, end_stream);\n        } else {\n            buffer_data(data);  // Wait for upstream connection\n        }\n    }\n\n    // Callback when upstream connection is ready\n    void onPoolReady(std::unique_ptr<GenericUpstream>&& upstream,\n                     HostDescriptionConstSharedPtr host) {\n        upstream_encoder_ = upstream->newStream(this);  // Get encoder\n        upstream_encoder_->encodeHeaders(request_headers_, end_stream_);\n        if (buffered_data_) {\n            upstream_encoder_->encodeData(*buffered_data_, ...);\n        }\n    }\n\n    // Callback when upstream connection fails\n    void onPoolFailure(PoolFailureReason reason, ...) {\n        parent_.onUpstreamReset(reason);  // Trigger retry or error response\n    }\n\n    // Response arrives from upstream\n    void decodeHeaders(ResponseHeaderMapPtr&& headers, bool end_stream) {\n        parent_.onUpstreamHeaders(response_code, headers, ...);\n    }\n};\n```\n\n### Upstream Response Handling\n\nWhen upstream sends response:\n\n```\nUpstreamRequest.decodeHeaders(upstream_response_headers)\n  └─ UpstreamCodecFilter (last filter in upstream chain) receives headers\n      └─ Passes to UpstreamRequest's callback (via filter manager)\n          └─ UpstreamRequest.decodeHeaders()\n              └─ Router.onUpstreamHeaders()\n                  └─ Call downstream encoder (ActiveStream.response_encoder_)\n                      └─ Encoder passes through encoder filter chain (reverse order)\n                          └─ Downstream codec encodes to wire\n```\n\n### Retry and Timeout Handling\n\nUpstreamRequest manages:\n\n1. **Retries**: If upstream resets with retriable status (5xx), create new UpstreamRequest\n   - Configured via route's `RetryPolicy`\n   - Respects retry count limits\n\n2. **Per-try timeout**: Timer for each upstream attempt\n   - If expired, fail this attempt and trigger retry or final error response\n\n3. **Request timeout**: Timer for entire downstream request-response\n   - If expired before receiving full response, return 504 Gateway Timeout\n\n4. **Hedged requests** (optional):\n   - Send duplicate requests to multiple hosts in parallel\n   - Use response from whichever arrives first\n\n### Data Flow Summary\n\n```\nDownstream Request:\n  Codec.dispatch(data)\n    → ActiveStream.decodeHeaders()\n      → FilterManager.decodeHeaders()\n        → [Filter chain: A.decodeHeaders → B.decodeHeaders → Router.decodeHeaders]\n          → Router initiates upstream via UpstreamRequest\n\n  Codec.dispatch(data)  // more data\n    → ActiveStream.decodeData()\n      → FilterManager.decodeData()\n        → [Filter chain: A.decodeData → B.decodeData → Router.decodeData]\n          → UpstreamRequest.acceptDataFromRouter()\n            → Upstream codec encodes and sends\n\nUpstream Response:\n  Upstream codec (via pool)\n    → UpstreamRequest.decodeHeaders()\n      → UpstreamFilterManager.encodeHeaders()  (upstream filters)\n        → [Upstream filters in reverse]\n          → UpstreamRequest callback\n            → Router.onUpstreamHeaders()\n              → ActiveStream.response_encoder_.encodeHeaders()\n                → FilterManager.encodeHeaders()  (downstream filters)\n                  → [Filter chain in reverse: Router.encodeHeaders → B.encodeHeaders → A.encodeHeaders]\n                    → Downstream codec encodes to wire\n```\n\n---\n\n## 4. Cluster Manager and Upstream Connectivity\n\n**Source files:**\n- `source/common/upstream/cluster_manager_impl.h` (lines 52-200)\n- `source/common/upstream/cluster_manager_impl.cc` (lines 1-300)\n\n### Responsibilities\n\nClusterManagerImpl provides:\n\n- **Cluster state management**: owns all upstream clusters, their health status, load balancers\n- **Thread-local cluster access**: via `ThreadLocalCluster` for connection pool allocation\n- **Connection pool creation**: allocates HTTP or TCP pools per cluster/host combination\n- **Load balancing**: coordinates load balancer selection of hosts\n- **Health checking and outlier detection**: feeds back into load balancer decisions\n\n### Architecture: ThreadLocal Access Pattern\n\nClusterManagerImpl uses thread-local storage for performance (avoiding locks on hot path):\n\n```cpp\nclass ClusterManagerImpl {\n    struct ThreadLocalClusterManagerImpl : public ThreadLocal::ThreadLocalObject {\n        // Per-thread state for each cluster\n        std::unordered_map<std::string, ClusterEntry> clusters_;\n\n        struct ClusterEntry {\n            Cluster& cluster_;                    // Shared cluster\n            LoadBalancer& load_balancer_;         // Per-thread LB instance\n            PriorityConnPoolMap<...> conn_pools_; // HTTP pools per host/priority\n            std::map<...> tcp_pools_;            // TCP pools per host\n        };\n    };\n\n    ThreadLocal::SlotPtr tls_;  // Slot for ThreadLocalClusterManagerImpl\n};\n```\n\n### Getting a Connection Pool\n\nWhen Router needs to send upstream request:\n\n```cpp\n// 1. Get thread-local cluster\nUpstream::ThreadLocalCluster* thread_local_cluster =\n    cluster_manager_.getThreadLocalCluster(cluster_name);\n\n// 2. Get connection pool from thread-local cluster\nauto conn_pool_data = thread_local_cluster->httpConnPool(\n    priority,                    // ResourcePriority::Default, etc.\n    protocol,                    // Http::Protocol::Http11, Http2, Http3\n    context                      // LoadBalancerContext (with metadata match, etc.)\n);\n\n// 3. Allocate new stream\nauto stream_encoder = conn_pool_data.pool_->newStream(*upstream_request_callbacks);\n\n// 4. If pool has available connection, newStream() calls onPoolReady() immediately\n//    Otherwise, queues request and calls onPoolReady() once connection available\n```\n\n### Connection Pool Lifecycle\n\n```\nClusterManagerImpl.allocateConnPool()  (called from ConnPoolDataImpl)\n  ├─ Create Http::ConnectionPool::Instance\n  │   ├─ Owns connections to a specific host\n  │   ├─ Maintains FIFO queue of pending requests\n  │   ├─ Manages connection limits (max connections per host)\n  │   └─ Implements HTTP/1 connection reuse (persistent connections)\n  │\n  └─ Return pool to thread-local cluster\n\npool_->newStream()\n  ├─ If idle connection available:\n  │   ├─ Get RequestEncoder from that connection\n  │   ├─ Call newStream callback immediately\n  │   └─ Caller can send request immediately\n  │\n  └─ Else if connections < max:\n  │   ├─ Create new connection to host (async)\n  │   ├─ Queue pending stream request\n  │   └─ When connection established, provision encoder and call callback\n  │\n  └─ Else (at limit):\n      ├─ Queue pending stream request\n      └─ When connection becomes idle, service from queue\n```\n\n### Load Balancing\n\nWhen Router calls `httpConnPool()`, ClusterManager coordinates:\n\n```cpp\n// In thread-local cluster:\nhttpConnPool(..., context /* LoadBalancerContext */) {\n    // 1. Load balancer selects host\n    auto host = load_balancer_.chooseHost(context);\n    if (!host) {\n        return onPoolFailure(NoHealthyUpstream);\n    }\n\n    // 2. Get or create pool for that host\n    auto pool = getPriorityPool(host, priority);\n\n    // 3. Return pool with selected host info\n    return HttpPoolData{pool, host};\n}\n```\n\n**LoadBalancer implementations:**\n- Round robin: cycle through healthy hosts\n- Least request: send to host with fewest active connections\n- Ring hash: hash-based with consistent hashing (for session affinity)\n- Custom: user-provided load balancer extension\n\n### Health Checking and Outlier Detection\n\nClusterManager integrates:\n\n1. **Health checks**: Active health check probes (HTTP, TCP, or gRPC)\n   - Mark hosts as healthy/unhealthy\n   - Feed status to load balancer\n\n2. **Outlier detection**: Passive observation of request failures\n   - Detect hosts sending excessive errors\n   - Temporarily eject them from rotation\n   - Periodic re-attempts to bring them back\n\nLoad balancer receives updated host status and excludes failing hosts from selection.\n\n### Connection Pool Isolation\n\nPools are isolated by:\n\n1. **Host** — separate pool per upstream host\n2. **Priority** — separate pools for different priorities (e.g., default vs. high)\n3. **Protocol** — separate pools for HTTP/1, HTTP/2, HTTP/3\n\nThis allows:\n- Per-host connection limits\n- Separate circuit breaking per priority\n- Protocol-specific connection pooling (multiplexing in HTTP/2 vs. separate connections in HTTP/1)\n\n---\n\n## Request Path: Complete Data Flow\n\n### Downstream Request to Upstream Dispatch\n\n```\n1. Downstream TCP Connection\n   Network layer → onNewConnection()\n\n2. First Bytes Arrive\n   Network layer → onData(Buffer)\n   └─ ConnectionManagerImpl.onData()\n       ├─ Create codec (detect H1/H2/H3)\n       └─ codec_→dispatch(data)\n           └─ Codec parses frame(s), calls newStream() for each request\n\n3. New HTTP Request\n   Codec → ConnectionManagerImpl.newStream()\n   └─ Create ActiveStream\n       ├─ Create FilterManager\n       ├─ Create decoder filter chain via FilterChainFactory\n       └─ Return RequestDecoder to codec\n\n4. Request Headers Arrive\n   Codec → ActiveStream.decodeHeaders(headers, end_stream=false)\n   └─ FilterManager.decodeHeaders()\n       ├─ Iterate filters [A, B, ..., Router]:\n       │   └─ A.decodeHeaders()\n       │       └─ B.decodeHeaders()\n       │           └─ ...\n       │               └─ Router.decodeHeaders()\n       │                   ├─ Select route\n       │                   ├─ Select cluster\n       │                   └─ Create UpstreamRequest\n       │                       └─ Request connection from ClusterManager\n       └─ Return StopIteration (wait for upstream)\n\n5. Upstream Connection Pool Allocation\n   ClusterManager.getThreadLocalCluster(cluster)\n   ├─ Get thread-local instance\n   ├─ Select load balancer picks host\n   ├─ Return or create HTTP::ConnectionPool for host\n   └─ pool_→newStream(upstream_request_callbacks)\n\n6. Upstream Connection Ready (or queued)\n   ConnectionPool → UpstreamRequest.onPoolReady()\n   └─ Get request encoder\n       └─ Encode downstream request headers to upstream\n\n7. Request Body Arrives Downstream\n   Codec → ActiveStream.decodeData(data, end_stream=false)\n   └─ FilterManager.decodeData()\n       ├─ [Filter chain iteration]\n       └─ Router.decodeData()\n           └─ UpstreamRequest.acceptDataFromRouter()\n               └─ upstream_encoder_→encodeData(data, end_stream)\n\n8. Request Trailers Arrive (or end_stream=true on final data)\n   [Similar to step 4 or 7]\n   └─ Router.decodeTrailers()\n       └─ upstream_encoder_→encodeTrailers()\n           └─ Upstream receives complete request\n```\n\n### Upstream Response to Downstream Delivery\n\n```\n9. Upstream Sends Response\n   Upstream codec (in conn pool) → UpstreamRequest.decodeHeaders()\n   └─ UpstreamFilterManager.encodeHeaders()  (upstream-side filters)\n       ├─ Upstream filters in reverse order\n       └─ Final callback\n           └─ Router.onUpstreamHeaders()\n               └─ Call response_encoder_→encodeHeaders()\n                   └─ ActiveStream.response_encoder_.encodeHeaders()\n                       └─ FilterManager.encodeHeaders()  (downstream filters)\n                           ├─ [Filter chain in reverse: Router, ..., B, A]\n                           └─ A.encodeHeaders()\n                               └─ Downstream codec.encodeHeaders()\n                                   └─ Write HTTP response status + headers to downstream TCP\n\n10. Response Body Arrives\n    Upstream codec → UpstreamRequest.decodeData()\n    └─ UpstreamFilterManager.encodeData()\n        └─ Router.onUpstreamData()\n            └─ FilterManager.encodeData() [downstream direction]\n                └─ [Downstream filter chain]\n                    └─ Downstream codec.encodeData()\n                        └─ Write response body to downstream TCP\n\n11. Response Complete\n    Upstream codec → UpstreamRequest.decodeTrailers() or decodeData(end_stream=true)\n    └─ [Similar to step 10]\n    └─ ActiveStream marked complete\n    └─ Deferred delete of ActiveStream\n\n12. Connection Reuse (if keep-alive)\n    Pool returns connection to idle list\n    Next queued request gets encoder from same connection\n```\n\n---\n\n## Error Handling\n\n### Codec Errors\n\nIf HTTP codec detects invalid message (malformed headers, etc.):\n\n```\nCodec::dispatch() detects error\n  ├─ In H1: call onError() callback in CodecEventCallbacks\n  │   └─ ActiveStream::onCodecLowLevelReset()\n  │       └─ Send local reply (400 Bad Request)\n  │\n  └─ In H2: RST_STREAM with error code\n      └─ Stream reset callback\n          └─ Inform filter chain (onResetStream)\n```\n\nIf downstream connection has protocol error, close connection immediately.\n\n### Filter Chain Errors\n\nIf a filter returns `StopIteration` and never resumes:\n\n```\nFilter is configured to resume on upstream pool ready\n  └─ Pool calls onPoolReady()\n      └─ RouterFilter.onUpstreamReady()\n          └─ Calls filter's resumeIteration()\n\nIf filter is still blocked:\n  ├─ Router timeout expires (per-try-timeout, request-timeout)\n  └─ Send local reply (504 Gateway Timeout or context-appropriate error)\n```\n\n### Upstream Connection Failures\n\nIf upstream connection fails:\n\n```\nUpstreamRequest.onPoolFailure(reason)\n  ├─ If reason is retriable and retries remain:\n  │   ├─ Create new UpstreamRequest\n  │   └─ Request new connection from pool\n  │\n  ├─ Else if reason is connection timeout:\n  │   └─ Send local reply (504 Gateway Timeout)\n  │\n  ├─ Else if cluster has no healthy hosts:\n  │   └─ Send local reply (503 Service Unavailable)\n  │\n  └─ Else (other errors):\n      └─ Send local reply (502 Bad Gateway or context-specific)\n```\n\nRetries are limited by:\n- `max_retries` in route's RetryPolicy\n- Retriable status codes (5xx, 429, reset)\n- Per-try timeout (don't retry if per-try timeout expires)\n\n---\n\n## Extension Points\n\nUsers extend HCM via:\n\n### 1. HTTP Filters\n\nImplement `StreamDecoderFilter`, `StreamEncoderFilter`, or `StreamFilter`:\n\n```cpp\nclass CustomFilter : public Http::StreamFilter {\npublic:\n    FilterHeadersStatus decodeHeaders(RequestHeaderMap& headers, bool end_stream) override {\n        // Modify headers, make async calls, stop iteration, etc.\n    }\n\n    FilterDataStatus decodeData(Buffer::Instance& data, bool end_stream) override {\n        // Buffer or process body\n    }\n\n    FilterHeadersStatus encodeHeaders(ResponseHeaderMap& headers, bool end_stream) override {\n        // Modify response headers\n    }\n};\n```\n\nRegister in HCM config:\n```yaml\nhttp_filters:\n  - name: envoy.filters.http.my_custom_filter\n```\n\n### 2. Cluster Extensions\n\nImplement custom cluster type (e.g., custom service discovery):\n\n```cpp\nclass CustomClusterFactory : public ClusterFactory {\n    clusterFromProto(const Cluster& config) override {\n        return std::make_unique<CustomCluster>(config);\n    }\n};\n```\n\n### 3. Load Balancer Extensions\n\nImplement custom load balancing algorithm:\n\n```cpp\nclass CustomLoadBalancer : public LoadBalancer {\n    HostConstSharedPtr chooseHost(LoadBalancerContext* context) override {\n        // Custom host selection logic\n    }\n};\n```\n\n### 4. Route Configuration\n\nSpecify routes in bootstrap config or via RDS (Route Discovery Service):\n\n```protobuf\nroutes:\n  - name: default\n    virtual_hosts:\n      - name: backend\n        domains: [\"example.com\"]\n        routes:\n          - match:\n              prefix: \"/api\"\n            route:\n              cluster: api-cluster\n          - match:\n              prefix: \"/\"\n            route:\n              cluster: www-cluster\n```\n\n### 5. Access Logging\n\nImplement custom access logger:\n\n```cpp\nclass CustomAccessLog : public AccessLog::Instance {\n    void log(AccessLogType, const StreamInfo::StreamInfo& info) override {\n        // Log request/response details\n    }\n};\n```\n\nRegister and specify in HCM config:\n```yaml\naccess_logs:\n  - name: envoy.access_loggers.my_logger\n    typed_config:\n      \"@type\": type.googleapis.com/my.custom.AccessLog\n```\n\n---\n\n## Key Design Decisions\n\n### 1. Lazy Codec Creation\nH1/H2 codecs are created on first data arrival, not on connection establishment. This defers memory allocation until needed. H3 is created immediately because QUIC has out-of-order delivery.\n\n### 2. Filter Chain Reversal for Encoder\nThe encoder chain runs in reverse order of the decoder chain. This ensures the last decoder filter (Router) is also the last to see outgoing response, allowing it to make final modifications.\n\n### 3. Thread-Local Cluster Manager\nUsing thread-local storage avoids lock contention on the critical path. ClusterManager provides thread-safe access via a thread-local slot pattern.\n\n### 4. Per-Host Connection Pools\nIsolating connection pools by host allows per-host circuit breaking and connection limits without blocking traffic to healthy hosts.\n\n### 5. Async Upstream Request Initiation\nUpstream request creation is async (returns `StopIteration`). The router doesn't wait for connection to be ready; it resumes decoding once the connection pool provides an encoder.\n\n### 6. Active Health Checking and Outlier Detection\nClusterManager decouples connection management from health status. Health checks and outlier detection feed back into load balancer decisions without requiring changes to pools or routers.\n\n---\n\n## Relevant Source Files\n\n### Core Components\n- `source/common/http/conn_manager_impl.h/cc` — ConnectionManagerImpl\n- `source/common/http/filter_manager.h/cc` — FilterManager and filter chain\n- `source/common/router/router.h/cc` — Router filter\n- `source/common/router/upstream_request.h/cc` — Upstream request lifecycle\n- `source/common/upstream/cluster_manager_impl.h/cc` — ClusterManager\n\n### Codecs\n- **ConnectionManagerImpl** receives raw TCP bytes and provides the foundation for HTTP protocol handling, managing the connection lifecycle and creating codecs.\n\n2. **FilterManager** orchestrates per-stream filtering, creating filter chains and controlling iteration through decoders (request) and encoders (response).\n\n3. **Router Filter** is the terminal filter that selects upstream clusters and initiates upstream requests via UpstreamRequest.\n\n4. **Cluster Manager** abstracts upstream connectivity, providing connection pools, host selection via load balancers, and health-aware routing.\n\nTogether, these components handle the complete journey of an HTTP request from a downstream client through the filter chain to upstream dispatch, and the response back through filters to the downstream codec. The architecture supports extensive customization via filters, cluster extensions, and load balancer algorithms while maintaining performance through lazy initialization, thread-local access patterns, and efficient buffering.\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":12,"cache_creation_input_tokens":3366,"cache_read_input_tokens":77035,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":3366},"output_tokens":4,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"3160cdc5-ba1a-4ec5-a3d5-83cb8af4ed26","uuid":"50f5a67c-aa3c-4022-8e0e-ed13497ed99f"}

This document explains how the major components interact to handle HTTP request/response lifecycle: from receiving raw bytes on a downstream connection, through per-stream filtering and routing, to dispatching upstream requests and returning responses downstream.\n\nThe architecture consists of four tightly-integrated layers:\n\n1. **ConnectionManagerImpl** — Network I/O and connection lifecycle management\n2. **FilterManager** — Per-stream filter chain execution engine\n3. **Router Filter** — Terminal filter that performs route selection and upstream dispatch\n4. **Cluster Manager** — Upstream connection pool allocation and host selection\n\n---\n\n## 1. ConnectionManagerImpl: Network Read Filter and Connection Lifecycle\n\n**Source files:**\n- `source/common/http/conn_manager_impl.h` (lines 60-220)\n- `source/common/http/conn_manager_impl.cc` (lines 118-300)\n\n### Responsibilities\n\nConnectionManagerImpl is a `Network::ReadFilter` that owns the HTTP connection lifecycle. It:\n\n- **Receives raw downstream bytes** via the `Network::ReadFilter` interface's `onData()` method\n- **Instantiates and manages the HTTP codec** (H1/H2/H3) lazily based on the first bytes received\n- **Creates and tracks `ActiveStream` objects** — one per HTTP request/response pair\n- **Manages connection-level concerns**:\n  - Drain decisions (graceful shutdown)\n  - Overload management (rejecting new streams under load)\n  - Write buffer watermarks (pausing/resuming downstream read when buffers exceed limits)\n  - Connection lifetime limits (max requests, timeouts)\n  - Tracing and access logging coordination\n\n### Key Data Structures\n\n```cpp\nclass ConnectionManagerImpl :\n    public Network::ReadFilter,           // Implements onData()\n    public ServerConnectionCallbacks,     // Codec callbacks\n    public Network::ConnectionCallbacks   // Connection events\n{\nprivate:\n    struct ActiveStream : LinkedObject<ActiveStream>,     // Linked list node\n                         public FilterManagerCallbacks,   // Filter manager interface\n                         public StreamCallbacks          // Stream callbacks\n    {\n        // Per-stream state:\n        RequestHeaderMapSharedPtr request_headers_;\n        ResponseHeaderMapPtr response_headers_;\n        uint32_t stream_id_;\n        FilterManager filter_manager_;                    // Stream's filter chain\n        // ... additional stream state\n    };\n\n    ServerConnectionPtr codec_;           // HTTP codec (created lazily)\n    std::list<ActiveStream> active_streams_;  // Linked list of streams\n    Network::ReadFilterCallbacks* read_callbacks_;\n};\n```\n\n### Connection Lifecycle: From Bytes to Streams\n\n#### 1. Connection Established\n```\nNetwork → onNewConnection()\n  ├─ Register connection callbacks with Network::Connection\n  └─ Defer codec creation (H1/H2 wait for first bytes, H3 creates immediately)\n```\n\n#### 2. Downstream Bytes Arrive\n```\nNetwork → onData(Buffer::Instance& data)\n  ├─ Check if codec exists; if not, createCodec(data)\n  │   └─ Codec creation:\n  │       ├─ Inspect first bytes to determine protocol\n  │       ├─ Instantiate Http1CodecImpl, Http2CodecImpl, or Http3CodecImpl\n  │       └─ Register this as ServerConnectionCallbacks\n  │\n  └─ Dispatch data to codec:\n      codec_->dispatch(data)\n          └─ Codec parses frames and calls newStream() for each request\n```\n\n#### 3. Codec Signals New Request\n```\nCodec → newStream(ResponseEncoder& response_encoder)\n  ├─ Create ActiveStream in active_streams_ list\n  ├─ Allocate RequestDecoder interface from ActiveStream\n  └─ Return RequestDecoder to codec\n      └─ Codec calls decoder→decodeHeaders(), decodeData(), decodeTrailers()\n```\n\n### ActiveStream: Per-Stream Filtering and Response\n\nEach `ActiveStream`:\n\n- **Acts as RequestDecoder**: Receives decoded headers/data/trailers from the codec\n- **Owns a FilterManager**: Manages the per-stream filter chain\n- **Implements FilterManagerCallbacks**: Callbacks from FilterManager to coordinate response sending\n- **Implements StreamCallbacks**: Receives codec-level events (reset, watermarks)\n\n```cpp\nstruct ActiveStream : RequestDecoder, FilterManagerCallbacks {\n\n    // From codec: decoded request data\n    void decodeHeaders(RequestHeaderMapSharedPtr&& headers, bool end_stream) {\n        filter_manager_.decodeHeaders(*headers, end_stream);  // Send through filter chain\n    }\n\n    void decodeData(Buffer::Instance& data, bool end_stream) {\n        filter_manager_.decodeData(data, end_stream);         // Send through filter chain\n    }\n\n    void decodeTrailers(RequestTrailerMapPtr&& trailers) {\n        filter_manager_.decodeTrailers(*trailers);           // Send through filter chain\n    }\n\n    // From filter chain: response to send\n    void encodeHeaders(ResponseHeaderMapPtr&& headers, bool end_stream) override {\n        response_encoder_->encodeHeaders(*headers, end_stream);  // Codec encodes to wire\n    }\n};\n```\n\n### Connection-Level Concerns\n\n#### Overload Management\n- Before accepting a new stream, check `OverloadManager::isOverloaded()`\n- If overloaded, send local reply with 503 Service Unavailable\n- Prevents unbounded stream accumulation under load\n\n#### Drain Decision\n- Checks `Network::DrainDecision` at connection level\n- When draining, sends GOAWAY (HTTP/2) or closes after final response\n- Allows graceful load balancer-initiated shutdown\n\n#### Write Buffer Watermarking\n```\nFilter chain buffers response → watermark high\n  └─ Codec's write buffer exceeds limit\n      └─ ConnectionManagerImpl→onAboveWriteBufferHighWatermark()\n          └─ codec_→onUnderlyingConnectionAboveWriteBufferHighWatermark()\n              └─ Pauses new stream reads\n\nCodec flushes buffer → watermark low\n  └─ ConnectionManagerImpl→onBelowWriteBufferLowWatermark()\n      └─ codec_→onUnderlyingConnectionBelowWriteBufferLowWatermark()\n          └─ Resumes new stream reads\n```\n\n---\n\n## 2. FilterManager and HTTP Filter Chain\n\n**Source files:**\n- `source/common/http/filter_manager.h` (lines 679-850)\n- `source/common/http/filter_manager.cc`\n\n### Responsibilities\n\nFilterManager is the per-stream **filter chain execution engine**. It:\n\n- **Creates the filter chain** via `FilterChainFactory::createFilterChain()` for each new stream\n- **Routes data through decoder filters** (request path: headers → data → trailers)\n- **Routes data through encoder filters** (response path: same, in reverse order)\n- **Manages filter state transitions**: continuing, stopping, buffering, resuming\n- **Handles local replies**: sending error responses without involving upstream\n- **Coordinates watermarks**: pausing iteration when filters buffer data\n\n### Filter Chain Structure\n\n```cpp\n// Decoder filter chain: A → B → C (in configured order)\nstruct StreamDecoderFilters {\n    std::vector<ActiveStreamDecoderFilterPtr> entries_;  // A, B, C\n    Iterator begin() { return entries_.begin(); }       // Iterates A→B→C\n};\n\n// Encoder filter chain: A → B → C (in reverse order)\nstruct StreamEncoderFilters {\n    std::vector<ActiveStreamEncoderFilterPtr> entries_;  // A, B, C\n    using Iterator = reverse_iterator;\n    Iterator begin() { return entries_.rbegin(); }      // Iterates C→B→A\n};\n```\n\n**Why reverse iteration for encoder?**\nData flows: `Router → FilterN → … → Filter1 → Codec`\nEach layer can modify/observe response before it reaches prior layers.\nTerminal filter (Router) is executed last on the way out, giving it last chance to modify response.\n\n### Request Path: decodeHeaders → decodeData → decodeTrailers\n\n```\ndecodeHeaders(headers, end_stream=false)\n  └─ FilterManager::decodeHeaders()\n      ├─ Iterate decoder_filters: [A, B, C, Router]\n      │   ├─ A.decodeHeaders(headers) → Continue\n      │   ├─ B.decodeHeaders(headers) → Continue\n      │   ├─ C.decodeHeaders(headers) → Continue\n      │   └─ Router.decodeHeaders(headers) → [router selects upstream]\n      │\n      └─ If headers indicate end_stream=true, send to downstream now\n\ndecodeData(data, end_stream=false)\n  └─ FilterManager::decodeData()\n      ├─ Iterate decoder_filters: [A, B, C, Router]\n      │   ├─ A.decodeData(data) → Continue (or buffer)\n      │   ├─ B.decodeData(data) → Continue\n      │   ├─ C.decodeData(data) → Continue\n      │   └─ Router.decodeData(data) → [forward to upstream]\n      │\n      └─ If end_stream=true, downstream request complete\n\ndecodeTrailers(trailers)\n  └─ Similar to decodeData, Router.decodeTrailers() signals upstream completion\n```\n\n### Response Path: encodeHeaders → encodeData → encodeTrailers\n\n```\n[Upstream sends response]\n  └─ UpstreamRequest.decodeHeaders(response_headers, end_stream=false)\n      └─ FilterManager (upstream direction).encodeHeaders()\n          ├─ Iterate encoder_filters in reverse: [Router, C, B, A]\n          │   ├─ Router.encodeHeaders(response_headers) → Continue\n          │   ├─ C.encodeHeaders(response_headers) → Continue\n          │   ├─ B.encodeHeaders(response_headers) → Continue\n          │   └─ A.encodeHeaders(response_headers) → Continue\n          │\n          └─ Call response_encoder_→encodeHeaders() [Codec encodes to wire]\n\n[Similarly for encodeData, encodeTrailers]\n```\n\n### Filter Return Values and Control Flow\n\nEach filter's callback returns a status that controls iteration:\n\n```cpp\nenum class FilterHeadersStatus {\n    Continue,              // Call next filter immediately\n    StopIteration,         // Stop, wait for resumption\n    StopIterationAndWatermark,  // Stop + inform FilterManager to apply watermarks\n    ContinueAndEndStream,  // Final headers already sent downstream\n};\n\nenum class FilterDataStatus {\n    Continue,              // Call next filter immediately\n    StopIteration,         // Buffer data, wait for resumption\n    StopIterationAndWatermark,  // Stop + apply backpressure\n    Continue,              // (no change)\n};\n```\n\n### Example: Router Filter Handling\n\nWhen Router filter's `decodeHeaders()` is called:\n1. Selects route based on request headers (domain, path, etc.)\n2. Looks up cluster from route\n3. Initiates upstream request creation asynchronously\n4. Returns `StopIteration` — waits for upstream to provide response encoder\n5. Once upstream pool provides encoder:\n   - Resumes remaining filters if any were stopped\n   - Continues with `decodeData` and `decodeTrailers` from downstream\n\nIf Router encounters an error (no cluster found, cluster unhealthy):\n- Calls `sendLocalReply(503, \"Cluster not found\")`\n- This **short-circuits the filter chain** — no upstream request is made\n- Response is encoded directly via downstream codec\n\n### Buffering and Watermarks\n\nWhen a filter returns `StopIterationAndWatermark`:\n\n```cpp\n// Filter busy, can't process more data\nreturn FilterDataStatus::StopIterationAndWatermark;\n\n// FilterManager:\n// 1. Buffers the provided_data in filter's internal buffer\n// 2. Calls FilterManager callbacks to signal high watermark upstream\n// 3. Downstream codec pauses reads\n// 4. When filter is ready: resumeIteration() → re-inject buffered data\n\n// Filter later calls: resumeIteration()\n// → FilterManager re-injects buffered data to next filter\n// → If all filters pass, eventually reaches codec or upstream\n```\n\n### Extension Points\n\nUsers extend HTTP handling via:\n\n1. **StreamDecoderFilter**: Sees request, can modify headers/body, optionally stop iteration\n   - Example: rate limiting filter, header manipulation\n2. **StreamEncoderFilter**: Sees response, can modify status/headers/body\n   - Example: response header addition, body compression\n3. **StreamFilter**: Both decoder and encoder (single object for bidirectional processing)\n   - Example: tracing filter, logging filter\n\n```cpp\n// Custom filter registration in HCM config:\nhttp_filters:\n  - name: envoy.filters.http.router\n    typed_config:\n      \"@type\": type.googleapis.com/envoy.extensions.filters.http.router.v3.Router\n      upstream_http_filters:\n        - name: my-custom-filter\n```\n\n---\n\n## 3. Router Filter: Route Selection and Upstream Dispatch\n\n**Source files:**\n- `source/common/router/router.h` (lines 1-300)\n- `source/common/router/router.cc` (lines 1-400)\n- `source/common/router/upstream_request.h` (lines 67-200)\n\n### Responsibilities\n\nThe Router filter is the **terminal decoder filter** that:\n\n- **Selects a route** from `RouteConfiguration` based on request headers\n- **Picks a cluster** from the matched route\n- **Initiates upstream request creation** via ClusterManager\n- **Manages request lifecycle**: retry logic, timeouts, shadowing\n- **Handles upstream response**: passes response back through filter chain (encoder direction)\n\n### Request Processing: decodeHeaders\n\n```cpp\nclass Filter : public StreamDecoderFilter {\n    FilterHeadersStatus decodeHeaders(RequestHeaderMap& headers, bool end_stream) {\n        // 1. Route selection\n        route_entry_ = config_->routeConfig().route(headers, ...);\n        if (!route_entry_) {\n            sendLocalReply(Http::Code::NotFound, \"no matching route\");\n            return FilterHeadersStatus::StopIteration;\n        }\n\n        // 2. Cluster selection\n        cluster_ = route_entry_->clusterName();\n\n        // 3. Load balancer context setup\n        // (provides metadata match criteria, etc.)\n\n        // 4. Initiate upstream request\n        upstream_request_ = std::make_unique<UpstreamRequest>(\n            *this,\n            cluster_manager_.getThreadLocalCluster(cluster_)->connPool(...),\n            can_send_early_data_, can_use_http3_, enable_half_close\n        );\n\n        // 5. Pass headers to upstream pool\n        upstream_request_->acceptHeadersFromRouter(end_stream);\n\n        return FilterHeadersStatus::StopIteration;  // Wait for upstream pool\n    }\n};\n```\n\n### UpstreamRequest: Upstream Lifecycle\n\nUpstreamRequest (in `source/common/router/upstream_request.h`) manages the upstream side:\n\n```cpp\nclass UpstreamRequest {\n    // Connection pool obtained from cluster\n    std::unique_ptr<GenericConnPool> conn_pool_;\n\n    // Upstream encoder (once connection is ready)\n    Http::RequestEncoder* upstream_encoder_{nullptr};\n\n    // Filter manager for upstream-side filters\n    std::unique_ptr<Http::FilterManager> upstream_filter_manager_;\n\npublic:\n    // Called by router with downstream request data\n    void acceptHeadersFromRouter(bool end_stream) {\n        conn_pool_->newStream(*this);  // Async: calls onPoolReady() or onPoolFailure()\n    }\n\n    void acceptDataFromRouter(Buffer::Instance& data, bool end_stream) {\n        if (upstream_encoder_) {\n            upstream_encoder_->encodeData(data, end_stream);\n        } else {\n            buffer_data(data);  // Wait for upstream connection\n        }\n    }\n\n    // Callback when upstream connection is ready\n    void onPoolReady(std::unique_ptr<GenericUpstream>&& upstream,\n                     HostDescriptionConstSharedPtr host) {\n        upstream_encoder_ = upstream->newStream(this);  // Get encoder\n        upstream_encoder_->encodeHeaders(request_headers_, end_stream_);\n        if (buffered_data_) {\n            upstream_encoder_->encodeData(*buffered_data_, ...);\n        }\n    }\n\n    // Callback when upstream connection fails\n    void onPoolFailure(PoolFailureReason reason, ...) {\n        parent_.onUpstreamReset(reason);  // Trigger retry or error response\n    }\n\n    // Response arrives from upstream\n    void decodeHeaders(ResponseHeaderMapPtr&& headers, bool end_stream) {\n        parent_.onUpstreamHeaders(response_code, headers, ...);\n    }\n};\n```\n\n### Upstream Response Handling\n\nWhen upstream sends response:\n\n```\nUpstreamRequest.decodeHeaders(upstream_response_headers)\n  └─ UpstreamCodecFilter (last filter in upstream chain) receives headers\n      └─ Passes to UpstreamRequest's callback (via filter manager)\n          └─ UpstreamRequest.decodeHeaders()\n              └─ Router.onUpstreamHeaders()\n                  └─ Call downstream encoder (ActiveStream.response_encoder_)\n                      └─ Encoder passes through encoder filter chain (reverse order)\n                          └─ Downstream codec encodes to wire\n```\n\n### Retry and Timeout Handling\n\nUpstreamRequest manages:\n\n1. **Retries**: If upstream resets with retriable status (5xx), create new UpstreamRequest\n   - Configured via route's `RetryPolicy`\n   - Respects retry count limits\n\n2. **Per-try timeout**: Timer for each upstream attempt\n   - If expired, fail this attempt and trigger retry or final error response\n\n3. **Request timeout**: Timer for entire downstream request-response\n   - If expired before receiving full response, return 504 Gateway Timeout\n\n4. **Hedged requests** (optional):\n   - Send duplicate requests to multiple hosts in parallel\n   - Use response from whichever arrives first\n\n### Data Flow Summary\n\n```\nDownstream Request:\n  Codec.dispatch(data)\n    → ActiveStream.decodeHeaders()\n      → FilterManager.decodeHeaders()\n        → [Filter chain: A.decodeHeaders → B.decodeHeaders → Router.decodeHeaders]\n          → Router initiates upstream via UpstreamRequest\n\n  Codec.dispatch(data)  // more data\n    → ActiveStream.decodeData()\n      → FilterManager.decodeData()\n        → [Filter chain: A.decodeData → B.decodeData → Router.decodeData]\n          → UpstreamRequest.acceptDataFromRouter()\n            → Upstream codec encodes and sends\n\nUpstream Response:\n  Upstream codec (via pool)\n    → UpstreamRequest.decodeHeaders()\n      → UpstreamFilterManager.encodeHeaders()  (upstream filters)\n        → [Upstream filters in reverse]\n          → UpstreamRequest callback\n            → Router.onUpstreamHeaders()\n              → ActiveStream.response_encoder_.encodeHeaders()\n                → FilterManager.encodeHeaders()  (downstream filters)\n                  → [Filter chain in reverse: Router.encodeHeaders → B.encodeHeaders → A.encodeHeaders]\n                    → Downstream codec encodes to wire\n```\n\n---\n\n## 4. Cluster Manager and Upstream Connectivity\n\n**Source files:**\n- `source/common/upstream/cluster_manager_impl.h` (lines 52-200)\n- `source/common/upstream/cluster_manager_impl.cc` (lines 1-300)\n\n### Responsibilities\n\nClusterManagerImpl provides:\n\n- **Cluster state management**: owns all upstream clusters, their health status, load balancers\n- **Thread-local cluster access**: via `ThreadLocalCluster` for connection pool allocation\n- **Connection pool creation**: allocates HTTP or TCP pools per cluster/host combination\n- **Load balancing**: coordinates load balancer selection of hosts\n- **Health checking and outlier detection**: feeds back into load balancer decisions\n\n### Architecture: ThreadLocal Access Pattern\n\nClusterManagerImpl uses thread-local storage for performance (avoiding locks on hot path):\n\n```cpp\nclass ClusterManagerImpl {\n    struct ThreadLocalClusterManagerImpl : public ThreadLocal::ThreadLocalObject {\n        // Per-thread state for each cluster\n        std::unordered_map<std::string, ClusterEntry> clusters_;\n\n        struct ClusterEntry {\n            Cluster& cluster_;                    // Shared cluster\n            LoadBalancer& load_balancer_;         // Per-thread LB instance\n            PriorityConnPoolMap<...> conn_pools_; // HTTP pools per host/priority\n            std::map<...> tcp_pools_;            // TCP pools per host\n        };\n    };\n\n    ThreadLocal::SlotPtr tls_;  // Slot for ThreadLocalClusterManagerImpl\n};\n```\n\n### Getting a Connection Pool\n\nWhen Router needs to send upstream request:\n\n```cpp\n// 1. Get thread-local cluster\nUpstream::ThreadLocalCluster* thread_local_cluster =\n    cluster_manager_.getThreadLocalCluster(cluster_name);\n\n// 2. Get connection pool from thread-local cluster\nauto conn_pool_data = thread_local_cluster->httpConnPool(\n    priority,                    // ResourcePriority::Default, etc.\n    protocol,                    // Http::Protocol::Http11, Http2, Http3\n    context                      // LoadBalancerContext (with metadata match, etc.)\n);\n\n// 3. Allocate new stream\nauto stream_encoder = conn_pool_data.pool_->newStream(*upstream_request_callbacks);\n\n// 4. If pool has available connection, newStream() calls onPoolReady() immediately\n//    Otherwise, queues request and calls onPoolReady() once connection available\n```\n\n### Connection Pool Lifecycle\n\n```\nClusterManagerImpl.allocateConnPool()  (called from ConnPoolDataImpl)\n  ├─ Create Http::ConnectionPool::Instance\n  │   ├─ Owns connections to a specific host\n  │   ├─ Maintains FIFO queue of pending requests\n  │   ├─ Manages connection limits (max connections per host)\n  │   └─ Implements HTTP/1 connection reuse (persistent connections)\n  │\n  └─ Return pool to thread-local cluster\n\npool_->newStream()\n  ├─ If idle connection available:\n  │   ├─ Get RequestEncoder from that connection\n  │   ├─ Call newStream callback immediately\n  │   └─ Caller can send request immediately\n  │\n  └─ Else if connections < max:\n  │   ├─ Create new connection to host (async)\n  │   ├─ Queue pending stream request\n  │   └─ When connection established, provision encoder and call callback\n  │\n  └─ Else (at limit):\n      ├─ Queue pending stream request\n      └─ When connection becomes idle, service from queue\n```\n\n### Load Balancing\n\nWhen Router calls `httpConnPool()`, ClusterManager coordinates:\n\n```cpp\n// In thread-local cluster:\nhttpConnPool(..., context /* LoadBalancerContext */) {\n    // 1. Load balancer selects host\n    auto host = load_balancer_.chooseHost(context);\n    if (!host) {\n        return onPoolFailure(NoHealthyUpstream);\n    }\n\n    // 2. Get or create pool for that host\n    auto pool = getPriorityPool(host, priority);\n\n    // 3. Return pool with selected host info\n    return HttpPoolData{pool, host};\n}\n```\n\n**LoadBalancer implementations:**\n- Round robin: cycle through healthy hosts\n- Least request: send to host with fewest active connections\n- Ring hash: hash-based with consistent hashing (for session affinity)\n- Custom: user-provided load balancer extension\n\n### Health Checking and Outlier Detection\n\nClusterManager integrates:\n\n1. **Health checks**: Active health check probes (HTTP, TCP, or gRPC)\n   - Mark hosts as healthy/unhealthy\n   - Feed status to load balancer\n\n2. **Outlier detection**: Passive observation of request failures\n   - Detect hosts sending excessive errors\n   - Temporarily eject them from rotation\n   - Periodic re-attempts to bring them back\n\nLoad balancer receives updated host status and excludes failing hosts from selection.\n\n### Connection Pool Isolation\n\nPools are isolated by:\n\n1. **Host** — separate pool per upstream host\n2. **Priority** — separate pools for different priorities (e.g., default vs. high)\n3. **Protocol** — separate pools for HTTP/1, HTTP/2, HTTP/3\n\nThis allows:\n- Per-host connection limits\n- Separate circuit breaking per priority\n- Protocol-specific connection pooling (multiplexing in HTTP/2 vs. separate connections in HTTP/1)\n\n---\n\n## Request Path: Complete Data Flow\n\n### Downstream Request to Upstream Dispatch\n\n```\n1. Downstream TCP Connection\n   Network layer → onNewConnection()\n\n2. First Bytes Arrive\n   Network layer → onData(Buffer)\n   └─ ConnectionManagerImpl.onData()\n       ├─ Create codec (detect H1/H2/H3)\n       └─ codec_→dispatch(data)\n           └─ Codec parses frame(s), calls newStream() for each request\n\n3. New HTTP Request\n   Codec → ConnectionManagerImpl.newStream()\n   └─ Create ActiveStream\n       ├─ Create FilterManager\n       ├─ Create decoder filter chain via FilterChainFactory\n       └─ Return RequestDecoder to codec\n\n4. Request Headers Arrive\n   Codec → ActiveStream.decodeHeaders(headers, end_stream=false)\n   └─ FilterManager.decodeHeaders()\n       ├─ Iterate filters [A, B, ..., Router]:\n       │   └─ A.decodeHeaders()\n       │       └─ B.decodeHeaders()\n       │           └─ ...\n       │               └─ Router.decodeHeaders()\n       │                   ├─ Select route\n       │                   ├─ Select cluster\n       │                   └─ Create UpstreamRequest\n       │                       └─ Request connection from ClusterManager\n       └─ Return StopIteration (wait for upstream)\n\n5. Upstream Connection Pool Allocation\n   ClusterManager.getThreadLocalCluster(cluster)\n   ├─ Get thread-local instance\n   ├─ Select load balancer picks host\n   ├─ Return or create HTTP::ConnectionPool for host\n   └─ pool_→newStream(upstream_request_callbacks)\n\n6. Upstream Connection Ready (or queued)\n   ConnectionPool → UpstreamRequest.onPoolReady()\n   └─ Get request encoder\n       └─ Encode downstream request headers to upstream\n\n7. Request Body Arrives Downstream\n   Codec → ActiveStream.decodeData(data, end_stream=false)\n   └─ FilterManager.decodeData()\n       ├─ [Filter chain iteration]\n       └─ Router.decodeData()\n           └─ UpstreamRequest.acceptDataFromRouter()\n               └─ upstream_encoder_→encodeData(data, end_stream)\n\n8. Request Trailers Arrive (or end_stream=true on final data)\n   [Similar to step 4 or 7]\n   └─ Router.decodeTrailers()\n       └─ upstream_encoder_→encodeTrailers()\n           └─ Upstream receives complete request\n```\n\n### Upstream Response to Downstream Delivery\n\n```\n9. Upstream Sends Response\n   Upstream codec (in conn pool) → UpstreamRequest.decodeHeaders()\n   └─ UpstreamFilterManager.encodeHeaders()  (upstream-side filters)\n       ├─ Upstream filters in reverse order\n       └─ Final callback\n           └─ Router.onUpstreamHeaders()\n               └─ Call response_encoder_→encodeHeaders()\n                   └─ ActiveStream.response_encoder_.encodeHeaders()\n                       └─ FilterManager.encodeHeaders()  (downstream filters)\n                           ├─ [Filter chain in reverse: Router, ..., B, A]\n                           └─ A.encodeHeaders()\n                               └─ Downstream codec.encodeHeaders()\n                                   └─ Write HTTP response status + headers to downstream TCP\n\n10. Response Body Arrives\n    Upstream codec → UpstreamRequest.decodeData()\n    └─ UpstreamFilterManager.encodeData()\n        └─ Router.onUpstreamData()\n            └─ FilterManager.encodeData() [downstream direction]\n                └─ [Downstream filter chain]\n                    └─ Downstream codec.encodeData()\n                        └─ Write response body to downstream TCP\n\n11. Response Complete\n    Upstream codec → UpstreamRequest.decodeTrailers() or decodeData(end_stream=true)\n    └─ [Similar to step 10]\n    └─ ActiveStream marked complete\n    └─ Deferred delete of ActiveStream\n\n12. Connection Reuse (if keep-alive)\n    Pool returns connection to idle list\n    Next queued request gets encoder from same connection\n```\n\n---\n\n## Error Handling\n\n### Codec Errors\n\nIf HTTP codec detects invalid message (malformed headers, etc.):\n\n```\nCodec::dispatch() detects error\n  ├─ In H1: call onError() callback in CodecEventCallbacks\n  │   └─ ActiveStream::onCodecLowLevelReset()\n  │       └─ Send local reply (400 Bad Request)\n  │\n  └─ In H2: RST_STREAM with error code\n      └─ Stream reset callback\n          └─ Inform filter chain (onResetStream)\n```\n\nIf downstream connection has protocol error, close connection immediately.\n\n### Filter Chain Errors\n\nIf a filter returns `StopIteration` and never resumes:\n\n```\nFilter is configured to resume on upstream pool ready\n  └─ Pool calls onPoolReady()\n      └─ RouterFilter.onUpstreamReady()\n          └─ Calls filter's resumeIteration()\n\nIf filter is still blocked:\n  ├─ Router timeout expires (per-try-timeout, request-timeout)\n  └─ Send local reply (504 Gateway Timeout or context-appropriate error)\n```\n\n### Upstream Connection Failures\n\nIf upstream connection fails:\n\n```\nUpstreamRequest.onPoolFailure(reason)\n  ├─ If reason is retriable and retries remain:\n  │   ├─ Create new UpstreamRequest\n  │   └─ Request new connection from pool\n  │\n  ├─ Else if reason is connection timeout:\n  │   └─ Send local reply (504 Gateway Timeout)\n  │\n  ├─ Else if cluster has no healthy hosts:\n  │   └─ Send local reply (503 Service Unavailable)\n  │\n  └─ Else (other errors):\n      └─ Send local reply (502 Bad Gateway or context-specific)\n```\n\nRetries are limited by:\n- `max_retries` in route's RetryPolicy\n- Retriable status codes (5xx, 429, reset)\n- Per-try timeout (don't retry if per-try timeout expires)\n\n---\n\n## Extension Points\n\nUsers extend HCM via:\n\n### 1. HTTP Filters\n\nImplement `StreamDecoderFilter`, `StreamEncoderFilter`, or `StreamFilter`:\n\n```cpp\nclass CustomFilter : public Http::StreamFilter {\npublic:\n    FilterHeadersStatus decodeHeaders(RequestHeaderMap& headers, bool end_stream) override {\n        // Modify headers, make async calls, stop iteration, etc.\n    }\n\n    FilterDataStatus decodeData(Buffer::Instance& data, bool end_stream) override {\n        // Buffer or process body\n    }\n\n    FilterHeadersStatus encodeHeaders(ResponseHeaderMap& headers, bool end_stream) override {\n        // Modify response headers\n    }\n};\n```\n\nRegister in HCM config:\n```yaml\nhttp_filters:\n  - name: envoy.filters.http.my_custom_filter\n```\n\n### 2. Cluster Extensions\n\nImplement custom cluster type (e.g., custom service discovery):\n\n```cpp\nclass CustomClusterFactory : public ClusterFactory {\n    clusterFromProto(const Cluster& config) override {\n        return std::make_unique<CustomCluster>(config);\n    }\n};\n```\n\n### 3. Load Balancer Extensions\n\nImplement custom load balancing algorithm:\n\n```cpp\nclass CustomLoadBalancer : public LoadBalancer {\n    HostConstSharedPtr chooseHost(LoadBalancerContext* context) override {\n        // Custom host selection logic\n    }\n};\n```\n\n### 4. Route Configuration\n\nSpecify routes in bootstrap config or via RDS (Route Discovery Service):\n\n```protobuf\nroutes:\n  - name: default\n    virtual_hosts:\n      - name: backend\n        domains: [\"example.com\"]\n        routes:\n          - match:\n              prefix: \"/api\"\n            route:\n              cluster: api-cluster\n          - match:\n              prefix: \"/\"\n            route:\n              cluster: www-cluster\n```\n\n### 5. Access Logging\n\nImplement custom access logger:\n\n```cpp\nclass CustomAccessLog : public AccessLog::Instance {\n    void log(AccessLogType, const StreamInfo::StreamInfo& info) override {\n        // Log request/response details\n    }\n};\n```\n\nRegister and specify in HCM config:\n```yaml\naccess_logs:\n  - name: envoy.access_loggers.my_logger\n    typed_config:\n      \"@type\": type.googleapis.com/my.custom.AccessLog\n```\n\n---\n\n## Key Design Decisions\n\n### 1. Lazy Codec Creation\nH1/H2 codecs are created on first data arrival, not on connection establishment. This defers memory allocation until needed. H3 is created immediately because QUIC has out-of-order delivery.\n\n### 2. Filter Chain Reversal for Encoder\nThe encoder chain runs in reverse order of the decoder chain. This ensures the last decoder filter (Router) is also the last to see outgoing response, allowing it to make final modifications.\n\n### 3. Thread-Local Cluster Manager\nUsing thread-local storage avoids lock contention on the critical path. ClusterManager provides thread-safe access via a thread-local slot pattern.\n\n### 4. Per-Host Connection Pools\nIsolating connection pools by host allows per-host circuit breaking and connection limits without blocking traffic to healthy hosts.\n\n### 5. Async Upstream Request Initiation\nUpstream request creation is async (returns `StopIteration`). The router doesn't wait for connection to be ready; it resumes decoding once the connection pool provides an encoder.\n\n### 6. Active Health Checking and Outlier Detection\nClusterManager decouples connection management from health status. Health checks and outlier detection feed back into load balancer decisions without requiring changes to pools or routers.\n\n---\n\n## Relevant Source Files\n\n### Core Components\n- `source/common/http/conn_manager_impl.h/cc` — ConnectionManagerImpl\n- `source/common/http/filter_manager.h/cc` — FilterManager and filter chain\n- `source/common/router/router.h/cc` — Router filter\n- `source/common/router/upstream_request.h/cc` — Upstream request lifecycle\n- `source/common/upstream/cluster_manager_impl.h/cc` — ClusterManager\n\n### Codecs\n- `source/common/http/http1/codec_impl.h/cc` — HTTP/1 codec\n- `source/common/http/http2/codec_impl.h/cc` — HTTP/2 codec\n- `source/common/http/http3/codec_impl.h/cc` (quic) — HTTP/3 codec\n\n### Configuration\n- `source/common/http/conn_manager_config.h` — HCM configuration\n- `source/common/router/config_impl.h/cc` — Route configuration\n\n### Related Interfaces\n- `envoy/http/filter.h` — Filter base classes (StreamDecoderFilter, StreamEncoderFilter)\n- `envoy/http/codec.h` — Codec interfaces (Connection, RequestDecoder, ResponseEncoder)\n- `envoy/upstream/cluster_manager.h` — ClusterManager interface\n- `envoy/router/router_filter_interface.h` — Router interface\n\n---\n\n## Summary\n\nThe HTTP Connection Manager operates as a layered pipeline:\n\n1. **ConnectionManagerImpl** receives raw TCP bytes and provides the foundation for HTTP protocol handling, managing the connection lifecycle and creating codecs.\n\n2. **FilterManager** orchestrates per-stream filtering, creating filter chains and controlling iteration through decoders (request) and encoders (response).\n\n3. **Router Filter** is the terminal filter that selects upstream clusters and initiates upstream requests via UpstreamRequest.\n\n4. **Cluster Manager** abstracts upstream connectivity, providing connection pools, host selection via load balancers, and health-aware routing.\n\nTogether, these components handle the complete journey of an HTTP request from a downstream client through the filter chain to upstream dispatch, and the response back through filters to the downstream codec. The architecture supports extensive customization via filters, cluster extensions, and load balancer algorithms while maintaining performance through lazy initialization, thread-local access patterns, and efficient buffering.\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}

This document explains how the major components interact to handle HTTP request/response lifecycle: from receiving raw bytes on a downstream connection, through per-stream filtering and routing, to dispatching upstream requests and returning responses downstream.\n\nThe architecture consists of four tightly-integrated layers:\n\n1. **ConnectionManagerImpl** — Network I/O and connection lifecycle management\n2. **FilterManager** — Per-stream filter chain execution engine\n3. **Router Filter** — Terminal filter that performs route selection and upstream dispatch\n4. **Cluster Manager** — Upstream connection pool allocation and host selection\n\n---\n\n## 1. Async Upstream Request Initiation\nUpstream request creation is async (returns `StopIteration`). The router doesn't wait for connection to be ready; it resumes decoding once the connection pool provides an encoder.\n\n### 6. Active Health Checking and Outlier Detection\nClusterManager decouples connection management from health status. Health checks and outlier detection feed back into load balancer decisions without requiring changes to pools or routers.\n\n---\n\n## Relevant Source Files\n\n### Core Components\n- ClusterManager interface\n- `envoy/router/router_filter_interface.h` — Router interface\n\n---\n\n## Summary\n\nThe HTTP Connection Manager operates as a layered pipeline:\n\n1. **ConnectionManagerImpl** receives raw TCP bytes and provides the foundation for HTTP protocol handling, managing the connection lifecycle and creating codecs.\n\n2. **FilterManager** orchestrates per-stream filtering, creating filter chains and controlling iteration through decoders (request) and encoders (response).\n\n3. **Router Filter** is the terminal filter that selects upstream clusters and initiates upstream requests via UpstreamRequest.\n\n4. **Cluster Manager** abstracts upstream connectivity, providing connection pools, host selection via load balancers, and health-aware routing.\n\nTogether, these components handle the complete journey of an HTTP request from a downstream client through the filter chain to upstream dispatch, and the response back through filters to the downstream codec. The architecture supports extensive customization via filters, cluster extensions, and load balancer algorithms while maintaining performance through lazy initialization, thread-local access patterns, and efficient buffering.","stderr":"","interrupted":false,"isImage":false,"noOutputExpected":false}}
